# This file contains the setup effects for the tributaries in the game.
# The setup_tributaries_effect is invoked by on_game_start and should make calls to subsequent scripted effects.
# Sections are organized by top-suzerain title.
# Note that existing vassals (as established in title history) must be released and recreated into tributaries before
# they can have their own tributaries.



#I do not use Paradox's default setup as my map setup does not match theirs in any of the 3 bookmarks


setup_tributaries_effect = {

	#DLC enabled tribs - these are nomadic/herder tribs

	if = {
		limit = { has_mpo_dlc_trigger = yes	}

		if = {

# $TRIBUTARY$ = the new tributary
# $SUZERAIN$ = their suzerain
# $WAR$ = determines if this was caused by war or agreement, yes or no
break_subject_contract_and_establish_tributary_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { liege != this }
		create_title_and_vassal_change = {
			type = independency
			save_scope_as = change
			add_claim_on_loss = no
		}
		becomes_independent = {
			change = scope:change
		}
		resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:change
	}
	start_tributary_interaction_effect = {
		SUZERAIN = $SUZERAIN$
		TRIBUTARY = $TRIBUTARY$
	}
}


# Base game sets tribs by character which is a gigantic pain in the ass. It's more prone to typos, can't be easily copy and pasted between bookmarks, and requires you commenting everything so you know what the hell you're looking at. Doing my tribs by title similar to T4N
# Tribs of tribs DO work but they give an error that can be ignored. Annoyingly it doesn't seem like you can do confederations by title and are forced to use characters


############################################################################################################################	NOMADS/CONFEDERATIONS		############################################################################################################################
